# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy xDS v2 to v3 API Migration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement both xDS v2 and v3 API handling: the versioned proto type conversion, the v2-to-v3 field renames (e.g., DiscoveryRequest), and the dual-version subscription handling in the ADS gRPC server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)


68-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the xDS v2 and v3 API implementations in the Envoy repository. Here's what I found:

## Summary

I've identified **24 C++ source files** in envoyproxy/envoy that implement both xDS v2 and v3 API handling for the ADS gRPC server and dual-version subscription management.

### Key Findings:

**API Version Architecture:**
1. **Version Detection** - `source/common/config/utility.h` contains the critical `getVersionStringFromApiVersion()` function that validates and converts API versions, including deprecation warnings for v2
2. **Type URL Mapping** - `source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc` implements the reverse mapping from resource type URLs to v3 gRPC service methods
3. **ADS gRPC Implementations** - Multiple implementations in `grpc_mux_impl.cc` (legacy), `xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc` (unified), and `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc` (delta protocol)
4. **Subscription State Management** - Separate implementations for SotW (state-of-the-world) and Delta protocols in the `xds_mux/` subdirectory
5. **Factory Pattern** - `subscription_factory_impl.cc` routes subscriptions to appropriate implementations based on API version

**Dual-Version Support:**
- Configuration-time API version selection via ConfigSource protobuf
- Internal wire protocol standardization using v3 messages
- Graceful deprecation of v2 with warning logs
- Test evidence in `ads_integration_test.cc` showing v2 rejection by default

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed documentation including file paths, key symbols, call chains, and a comprehensive narrative explanation.

API shepherds are responsible for the execution of the xDS\\n85: day-to-day and guiding xDS implementation changes. Proposals from xDS-WG will be aligned with the\\n86: xDS API shepherds to ensure that xDS is heading towards the xDS goal of client and server neutral\\n87: xDS. xDS API shepherds operate under the [envoyproxy](https://github.com/envoyproxy) organization\\n88: but are expected to keep in mind the needs of all xDS clients (currently Envoy and gRPC, but we are\\n89: aware of other in-house implementations) and the goals of xDS-WG.\\n90: \\n91: If you wish to become an API shepherd and satisfy the above criteria, please contact an existing\\n92: API shepherd.             "content": "222: The following principles should be adhered to when extending or modifying the\n223: xDS APIs:\n224: \n225: * The xDS APIs have a logical distinction between transport and data model:\n226:   - The xDS transport protocol describes the network transport on which xDS\n227:     configuration resources are delivered to clients. A versioned gRPC streaming\n228:     protocol with support for ACK/NACK is provided by xDS; this is known as the\n229:     xDS transport protocol (xDS-TP). xDS configuration resources can also be\n230:     delivered on other transports, e.g. HTTP or filesystem, with some\n231: ",
            "endLine": 231,
            "startLine": 222
          },
          {
            "content": "234: \n235: * The xDS APIs are directionally client and server neutral. While many aspects\n236:   of the APIs reflect the history of their origin as Envoy's control plane APIs,\n237:   API decisions going forward should reflect the principle of client neutrality.\n238: \n239: * The xDS APIs are expressed canonically as [Proto3](https://developers.google.com/protocol-buffers/docs/proto3).\n240:   Both JSON and YAML are also supported formats, with the standard JSON-proto3\n241:   conversion used during client configuration ingestion.\n242: \n243: * xDS APIs are eventual consistency first. For example, if RDS references a\n244:   cluster that has not yet been supplied by CDS, it should be silently ignored\n245: ",
            "endLine": 245,
            "startLine": 234
          },
          {
            "content": "250: \n251: * The API is primarily intended for machine generation and consumption. It is\n252:   expected that the management server is responsible for mapping higher level\n253:   configuration concepts to API responses. Similarly, static configuration\n254:   fragments may be generated by templating tools, etc. With that consideration,\n255:   we also aim to have API artifacts readable by humans for debugging and\n256:   understanding applied configuration. This implies that APIs do not have to\n257:   have ergonomics as the main driver, but should still be reasonable to read by\n258:   humans. The APIs and tools used to generate xDS configuration are beyond the\n259:   scope of the definitions in this repository.\n260: ",

Subscription Factory (source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.cc/h)\\n\\nThe `SubscriptionFactoryImpl::subscriptionFromConfigSource()` method is the entry point for all subscription creation. ADS gRPC Mux Implementations\\n\\nThere are multiple ADS implementations supporting different subscription state protocols:\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.cc/h** (Legacy):\\n- The original ADS implementation supporting SotW (State-of-the-World) protocol\\n- `onDiscoveryResponse()` handles v3 DiscoveryResponse messages\\n- `sendDiscoveryRequest()` sends v3 DiscoveryRequest messages\\n- Uses the `apiStateFor()` method to manage per-type-url state\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc/h** (Unified):\\n- Newer unified implementation that can handle both SotW and Delta protocols\\n- Implements the abstraction with template parameters for different subscription state factories\\n- Validates local node information through `Config::Utility::checkLocalInfo(\\\"ads\\\", ...)`\\n- Creates appropriate subscription state objects through the factory\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h** (Delta-focused):\\n- Optimized for the Delta protocol\\n- Handles `DeltaDiscoveryResponse` directly\\n- Implements `onDiscoveryResponse()` for delta-specific processing\\n- Manages resource subscriptions and unsubscriptions\\n\\n#### 5. Subscription State Management\\n\\nThe subscription state classes handle the protocol-specific logic:\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc/h**:\\n- Manages SotW subscription state using v3 DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse\\n- Builds the next discovery request based on current subscription state\\n- Handles resource version tracking\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc/h**:\\n- Manages Delta subscription state using v3 DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse\\n- Tracks resource subscriptions/unsubscriptions\\n- Manages resource versions efficiently\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.cc/h** and **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h**:\\n- Support for individual subscriptions over ADS\\n- Handle pause/resume of subscriptions\\n- Watch management for resource updates\\n\\n#### 6. Watch Management (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.cc/h)\\n\\nManages the mapping between resource names and subscription callbacks, supporting dynamic addition and removal of watches for resource updates.\\n\\n### Dual-Version Support Architecture\\n\\nThe system implements dual-version support through:\\n\\n1. **Configuration-Time Version Selection**: The API version is determined from the ConfigSource protobuf message during subscription creation\\n\\n2. **Type URL Routing**: The `type_to_endpoint` module maps resource type URLs (which may refer to v2 types like \\\"type.googleapis.com/envoy.api.v2.Cluster\\\") to v3 service methods\\n\\n3. **Wire Protocol Standardization**: All internal communication uses v3 protobuf messages (DiscoveryRequest, DiscoveryResponse) regardless of the input API version\\n\\n4. **Deprecation Warning System**: When v2 transport API version is detected, the system logs warnings to encourage migration to v3\\n\\n### Test Evidence\\n\\n**test/integration/ads_integration_test.cc** contains:\\n- Test `DEPRECATED_FEATURE_TEST(RejectV2TransportConfigByDefault)` that validates v2 transport version rejection\\n- Configuration of resource_api_version and transport_api_version in test setup\\n- Demonstration of ADS message handling with v3 DiscoveryResponse\\n\\n### Summary\\n\\nThe xDS v2 to v3 API handling in Envoy is implemented through a sophisticated three-layer architecture:\\n1. **Configuration layer** that detects and validates API versions from ConfigSource messages\\n2. **Type mapping layer** that translates resource type URLs to appropriate service methods\\n3. **Protocol layer** that uses standardized v3 messages internally while supporting configuration of v2 (now deprecated and rejected by default)\\n\\nThe ADS gRPC server implementation in grpc_mux_impl.cc and its variants handle the dual-version subscription management through proper abstraction and state management, allowing seamless handling of both old v2 and current v3 API versions during the migration period.\"\n}\n",
